			set_country_flag = current_ddos
		}
		remove_effect = {

		}

			tag = SCO
			attack_bonus_against = 0.2
			breakthrough_bonus_against = 0.2
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = current_ddos
			}
		}
	}
	
	EAG_cyberexpropriation = {
		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 70
		cost = 0
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = current_ddos
			add_command_power = -50
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = current_ddos
			random_list = {
						50 = {
							random_owned_controlled_state = {
								add_building_construction = {
									type = industrial_complex
									level = 1
									instant_build = yes
								}
								add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
							}
						}
						50 = {
							random_owned_controlled_state = {
								add_building_construction = {
									type = arms_factory
									level = 1
									instant_build = yes
								}
								add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
							}
						}
					}
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = current_ddos
			}
			command_power > 50
		}
	}
